<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>In the previous tutorials text datatypes were explored such as the Immutable Unicode string, Immutable byte string and Mutable byte string the bytearray. These text datatypes were based upon the object class and were seen to have consistent data model identifiers. Python also has a number of numeric datatypes, this tutorial will focus on the immutable integer, which is a full number. </p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:advanced-gutenberg-blocks/summary -->

<!-- /wp:advanced-gutenberg-blocks/summary -->

<!-- wp:heading -->
<h2 class="wp-block-heading" id="dot-attributes-and-the-decimal-point">Dot Attributes and the Decimal Point</h2>
<!-- /wp:heading -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>When the text datatypes were explored a dot . was used to access attributes. For example:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>For numeric datatypes attributes can still be accessed from the instance name:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- /wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>For example:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"num.to_bytes()","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003enum.to_bytes()\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>b'c'</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>However if a dot attribute is attempted to be used from an integer, the dot is recognised by Python as a decimal point and instead of looking up an attribute for the integer 99, invalid characters are found following the decimal point in the floating point number 99.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"99.to_bytes()","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003e99.\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003eto_bytes()\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->
<div class="wp-block-kevinbatdorf-code-block-pro" style="font-size:.875rem;line-height:1.25rem"><span style="display:block;padding:16px 0 0 16px;margin-bottom:-1px;width:100%;text-align:left;background-color:#fff"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="54" height="14" viewBox="0 0 54 14"><g fill="none" fill-rule="evenodd" transform="translate(1 1)"><circle cx="6" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FF5F56" stroke="#E0443E" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="26" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FFBD2E" stroke="#DEA123" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="46" cy="6" r="6" fill="#27C93F" stroke="#1AAB29" stroke-width=".5"></circle></g></svg></span><span role="button" tabindex="0" data-code="99.to_bytes()" style="color:#24292e;display:none" aria-label="Copy" class="code-block-pro-copy-button"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="width:24px;height:24px" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path class="with-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m-6 9l2 2 4-4"></path><path class="without-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2"></path></svg></span><pre class="shiki github-light" style="background-color: #fff" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="color: #005CC5">99.</span><span style="color: #24292E">to_bytes()</span></span></code></pre></div>
<!-- /wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>SyntaxError: invalid decimal literal</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>As a consequence to the above, most of the identifiers used with numeric values are data model identifiers which typically map to numeric operators. Details about these identifiers can be seen when examining the help for the int class:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

 |  int(&#91;x]) -&gt; integer
 |  int(x, base=10) -&gt; integer
 |  
 |  Convert a number or string to an integer, or return 0 if no arguments
 |  are given.  If x is a number, return x.__int__().  For floating point
 |  numbers, this truncates towards zero.
 |

 |      length
 |        Length of bytes object to use.  An OverflowError is raised if the

 |        The byte order used to represent the integer.  If byteorder is 'big',
 |        the most significant byte is at the beginning of the byte array.  If
 |        byteorder is 'little', the most significant byte is at the end of the
 |        byte array.  To request the native byte order of the host system, use
 |        `sys.byteorder' as the byte order value.  Default is to use 'big'.

 |        If signed is False and a negative integer is given, an OverflowError

 |        Bytes and bytearray are examples of built-in objects that support the

 |        the most significant byte is at the beginning of the byte array.  If

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Notice that the return value shown above for each data model method shows how the function is typically invoked using a Python builtins function or operator.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The __getattribute__ data model defines the behaviour of the getattr builtins function which can be used to retrieve an attribute from an integer:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:heading -->
<h2 class="wp-block-heading" id="initialisation">Initialisation</h2>
<!-- /wp:heading -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Inputting int() will display the docstring of the initialisation signature of the integer class as a popup balloon. Some IDEs such as JupyterLab may require the keypress shift ⇧ and tab ↹ to invoke the docstring:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:enlighter/codeblock {"language":"raw","linenumbers":"false"} -->
<pre class="EnlighterJSRAW" data-enlighter-language="raw" data-enlighter-theme="" data-enlighter-highlight="" data-enlighter-linenumbers="false" data-enlighter-lineoffset="" data-enlighter-title="" data-enlighter-group="">Init signature:  int(self, /, *args, **kwargs)
Docstring:     
int([x]) -> integer
int(x, base=10) -> integer

Convert a number or string to an integer, or return 0 if no arguments
are given.  If x is a number, return x.__int__().  For floating point
numbers, this truncates towards zero.

If x is not a number or if base is given, then x must be a string,
bytes, or bytearray instance representing an integer literal in the
given base.  The literal can be preceded by '+' or '-' and be surrounded
by whitespace.  The base defaults to 10.  Valid bases are 0 and 2-36.
Base 0 means to interpret the base from the string as an integer literal.
>>> int('0b100', base=0)
4
Type:           type
Subclasses:     bool, IntEnum, IntFlag, _NamedIntConstant, Handle</pre>
<!-- /wp:enlighter/codeblock -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>An integer can be instantiated using:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<span class="line"><span style="color: #24292E">num</span></span></code></pre></div>
<!-- /wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>99</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>However since the integer is a fundamental datatype it is usually abbreviated as:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>99</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>An integer can also be created using a string:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"num = int('99', base=10)\nnum","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003enum \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003eint\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e(\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #032F62\u0022\u003e\u0026#39;99\u0026#39;\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e, \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #E36209\u0022\u003ebase\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003e10\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e)\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003enum\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->

<p>Recall that Hexadecimal values use the base 16.</p>

<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The hexadecimal string can be cast into an integer using:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:code -->

<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:heading -->
<h2 class="wp-block-heading" id="identifiers">Identifiers</h2>
<!-- /wp:heading -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>A list of identifiers can be seen from an integer instance:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:list -->
<ul><!-- wp:list-item -->
<li>as_integer_ratio</li>
<!-- /wp:list-item -->

<!-- wp:list-item -->
<li>bit_count</li>
<!-- /wp:list-item -->

<!-- wp:list-item -->
<li>bit_length</li>
<!-- /wp:list-item -->

<!-- wp:list-item -->
<li>conjugate</li>
<!-- /wp:list-item -->

<!-- wp:list-item -->
<li>denominator</li>
<!-- /wp:list-item -->

<!-- wp:list-item -->
<li>from_bytes</li>
<!-- /wp:list-item -->

<!-- wp:list-item -->
<li>imag</li>
<!-- /wp:list-item -->

<!-- wp:list-item -->
<li>numerator</li>
<!-- /wp:list-item -->

<!-- wp:list-item -->
<li>real</li>
<!-- /wp:list-item -->

<!-- wp:list-item -->
<li>to_bytes</li>
<!-- /wp:list-item --></ul>
<!-- /wp:list -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>These are grouped into fraction related identifiers:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:list -->
<ul><!-- wp:list-item -->
<li>numerator</li>
<!-- /wp:list-item -->

<!-- wp:list-item -->
<li>denominator</li>
<!-- /wp:list-item -->

<!-- wp:list-item -->
<li>as_integer_ratio </li>
<!-- /wp:list-item --></ul>
<!-- /wp:list -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>numerator and denominator are data descriptors which match the integer and are 1 respectively making the integer compatible with the Fraction class:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"num.numerator","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003enum.numerator\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The integer ratio returns the numerator and denominator within a tuple:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:enlighter/codeblock {"language":"raw","linenumbers":"false"} -->
<pre class="EnlighterJSRAW" data-enlighter-language="raw" data-enlighter-theme="" data-enlighter-highlight="" data-enlighter-linenumbers="false" data-enlighter-lineoffset="" data-enlighter-title="" data-enlighter-group="">Signature:  num.as_integer_ratio()
Docstring:
Return integer ratio.

Return a pair of integers, whose ratio is exactly equal to the original int
and with a positive denominator.

>>> (10).as_integer_ratio()
(10, 1)
>>> (-10).as_integer_ratio()
(-10, 1)
>>> (0).as_integer_ratio()
(0, 1)
Type:      builtin_function_or_method</pre>
<!-- /wp:enlighter/codeblock -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>from_bytes is an alternative constructor:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:enlighter/codeblock {"language":"raw","linenumbers":"false"} -->
<pre class="EnlighterJSRAW" data-enlighter-language="raw" data-enlighter-theme="" data-enlighter-highlight="" data-enlighter-linenumbers="false" data-enlighter-lineoffset="" data-enlighter-title="" data-enlighter-group="">Signature:  int.from_bytes(bytes, byteorder='big', *, signed=False)
Docstring:
Return the integer represented by the given array of bytes.

bytes
  Holds the array of bytes to convert.  The argument must either
  support the buffer protocol or be an iterable object producing bytes.
  Bytes and bytearray are examples of built-in objects that support the
  buffer protocol.
byteorder
  The byte order used to represent the integer.  If byteorder is 'big',
  the most significant byte is at the beginning of the byte array.  If
  byteorder is 'little', the most significant byte is at the end of the
  byte array.  To request the native byte order of the host system, use
  `sys.byteorder' as the byte order value.  Default is to use 'big'.
signed
  Indicates whether two's complement is used to represent the integer.
Type:      builtin_function_or_method</pre>
<!-- /wp:enlighter/codeblock -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The byte string b'hello' can be converted to an integer using:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"int.from_bytes(b'hello', byteorder='big')","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003eint\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e.from_bytes(\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003eb\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #032F62\u0022\u003e\u0026#39;hello\u0026#39;\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e, \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #E36209\u0022\u003ebyteorder\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #032F62\u0022\u003e\u0026#39;big\u0026#39;\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e)\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->
<div class="wp-block-kevinbatdorf-code-block-pro" style="font-size:.875rem;line-height:1.25rem"><span style="display:block;padding:16px 0 0 16px;margin-bottom:-1px;width:100%;text-align:left;background-color:#fff"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="54" height="14" viewBox="0 0 54 14"><g fill="none" fill-rule="evenodd" transform="translate(1 1)"><circle cx="6" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FF5F56" stroke="#E0443E" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="26" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FFBD2E" stroke="#DEA123" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="46" cy="6" r="6" fill="#27C93F" stroke="#1AAB29" stroke-width=".5"></circle></g></svg></span><span role="button" tabindex="0" data-code="int.from_bytes(b'hello', byteorder='big')" style="color:#24292e;display:none" aria-label="Copy" class="code-block-pro-copy-button"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="width:24px;height:24px" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path class="with-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m-6 9l2 2 4-4"></path><path class="without-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2"></path></svg></span><pre class="shiki github-light" style="background-color: #fff" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="color: #005CC5">int</span><span style="color: #24292E">.from_bytes(</span><span style="color: #D73A49">b</span><span style="color: #032F62">&#39;hello&#39;</span><span style="color: #24292E">, </span><span style="color: #E36209">byteorder</span><span style="color: #D73A49">=</span><span style="color: #032F62">&#39;big&#39;</span><span style="color: #24292E">)</span></span></code></pre></div>
<!-- /wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>448378203247</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>This can manually be calculated using the ordinal values for each character multiplied by powers of 256 (highest power to the right hand side - big endian):</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<p>For a little byteorder:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>478560413032</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>An unsigned byte ranges between 0 to 256, the mid value 128 can be examined:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"hex(128)","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003ehex\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e(\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003e128\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e)\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->

<!-- /wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>'0x80'</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>If the byte is signed this range is split between negative and positive values ranging from -128 to +128. The first 128 values (which incorporate the ASCII characters) are unchanged, the next 128 values take on positive values to 256 if unsigned or negative values if signed:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>128</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The to_bytes method is the reverse method and can be used to cast an integer into a bytes:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"num = 448378203247","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003enum \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003e448378203247\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->
<div class="wp-block-kevinbatdorf-code-block-pro" style="font-size:.875rem;line-height:1.25rem"><span style="display:block;padding:16px 0 0 16px;margin-bottom:-1px;width:100%;text-align:left;background-color:#fff"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="54" height="14" viewBox="0 0 54 14"><g fill="none" fill-rule="evenodd" transform="translate(1 1)"><circle cx="6" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FF5F56" stroke="#E0443E" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="26" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FFBD2E" stroke="#DEA123" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="46" cy="6" r="6" fill="#27C93F" stroke="#1AAB29" stroke-width=".5"></circle></g></svg></span><span role="button" tabindex="0" data-code="num = 448378203247" style="color:#24292e;display:none" aria-label="Copy" class="code-block-pro-copy-button"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="width:24px;height:24px" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path class="with-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m-6 9l2 2 4-4"></path><path class="without-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2"></path></svg></span><pre class="shiki github-light" style="background-color: #fff" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="color: #24292E">num </span><span style="color: #D73A49">=</span><span style="color: #24292E"> </span><span style="color: #005CC5">448378203247</span></span></code></pre></div>
<!-- /wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>It requires the length f the bytearray to be supplied as an input argument:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:enlighter/codeblock {"language":"raw","linenumbers":"false"} -->
<pre class="EnlighterJSRAW" data-enlighter-language="raw" data-enlighter-theme="" data-enlighter-highlight="" data-enlighter-linenumbers="false" data-enlighter-lineoffset="" data-enlighter-title="" data-enlighter-group="">Signature:  num.to_bytes(length=1, byteorder='big', *, signed=False)
Docstring:
Return an array of bytes representing an integer.

length
  Length of bytes object to use.  An OverflowError is raised if the
  integer is not representable with the given number of bytes.  Default
  is length 1.
byteorder
  The byte order used to represent the integer.  If byteorder is 'big',
  the most significant byte is at the beginning of the byte array.  If
  byteorder is 'little', the most significant byte is at the end of the
  byte array.  To request the native byte order of the host system, use
  `sys.byteorder' as the byte order value.  Default is to use 'big'.
signed
  Determines whether two's complement is used to represent the integer.
  If signed is False and a negative integer is given, an OverflowError
  is raised.
Type:      builtin_function_or_method</pre>
<!-- /wp:enlighter/codeblock -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Trailing zeros will be displayed if the length specified is larger:</p>

<p>An OverflowError will display if the int is too big for the specified length:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>OverflowError: int too big to convert</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The bit_length method returns the number of bits required to represent a number in binary:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:enlighter/codeblock {"language":"raw","linenumbers":"false"} -->
<pre class="EnlighterJSRAW" data-enlighter-language="raw" data-enlighter-theme="" data-enlighter-highlight="" data-enlighter-linenumbers="false" data-enlighter-lineoffset="" data-enlighter-title="" data-enlighter-group="">Signature:  num.bit_length()
Docstring:
Number of bits necessary to represent self in binary.

>>> bin(37)
'0b100101'
>>> (37).bit_length()
6
Type:      builtin_function_or_method</pre>
<!-- /wp:enlighter/codeblock -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>For example:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The binary representation of the number is:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>'0b10011'</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>There are 5 bits (shown after the 0b prefix):</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"num.bit_length()","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003enum.bit_length()\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->

<!-- /wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>5</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The bit_count, returns the number of these bits which have a value of 1:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:enlighter/codeblock {"language":"raw","linenumbers":"false"} -->
<pre class="EnlighterJSRAW" data-enlighter-language="raw" data-enlighter-theme="" data-enlighter-highlight="" data-enlighter-linenumbers="false" data-enlighter-lineoffset="" data-enlighter-title="" data-enlighter-group="">Signature:  num.bit_count()
Docstring:
Number of ones in the binary representation of the absolute value of self.

Also known as the population count.

>>> bin(13)
'0b1101'
>>> (13).bit_count()
3
Type:      builtin_function_or_method</pre>
<!-- /wp:enlighter/codeblock -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>In the example 3 of the values are 1:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"num.bit_count()","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003enum.bit_count()\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->

<!-- wp:heading -->
<h2 class="wp-block-heading" id="data-model-identifiers">Data Model Identifiers</h2>
<!-- /wp:heading -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The data model identifier __hash__ is defined for an integer, because an integer is hashable, the hash value is the integer itself:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>This means an integer can be used as a key in a mapping for example:</p>

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The data model method __index__ is also defined, meaning an integer can be used to index into a collection such as a Unicode string:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The formal representation of a string __repr__ is also defined:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"repr(num)","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003erepr\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e(num)\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>'19'</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Note because only the formal string representation __repr__ is defined, the informal string representation __str__ will behave identically:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"str(num)","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003estr\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e(num)\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>'19'</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The data model __format__ is defined which means the integer can be used in a formatted string, such as an fstring:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The __getnewargs__ data model identifier is used by the pickle module to pickle an integer into a byte string for transfer of data for example over a serial port:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>the pickled byte sequence contains details about the pickle protocol and uses the hex value of the integer:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:heading -->
<h2 class="wp-block-heading" id="unitary-data-model-identifiers">Unitary Data Model Identifiers</h2>
<!-- /wp:heading -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The unitary operator __pos__ defines the behaviour of the + operator. This returns the number unchanged:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"+num","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e+\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003enum\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->
<div class="wp-block-kevinbatdorf-code-block-pro" style="font-size:.875rem;line-height:1.25rem"><span style="display:block;padding:16px 0 0 16px;margin-bottom:-1px;width:100%;text-align:left;background-color:#fff"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="54" height="14" viewBox="0 0 54 14"><g fill="none" fill-rule="evenodd" transform="translate(1 1)"><circle cx="6" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FF5F56" stroke="#E0443E" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="26" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FFBD2E" stroke="#DEA123" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="46" cy="6" r="6" fill="#27C93F" stroke="#1AAB29" stroke-width=".5"></circle></g></svg></span><span role="button" tabindex="0" data-code="+num" style="color:#24292e;display:none" aria-label="Copy" class="code-block-pro-copy-button"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="width:24px;height:24px" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path class="with-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m-6 9l2 2 4-4"></path><path class="without-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2"></path></svg></span><pre class="shiki github-light" style="background-color: #fff" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="color: #D73A49">+</span><span style="color: #24292E">num</span></span></code></pre></div>
<!-- /wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>19</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The unitary operator __neg__ defines the behaviour when the - operator. The returned number has an inverted sign:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"-num","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e-\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003enum\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->
<div class="wp-block-kevinbatdorf-code-block-pro" style="font-size:.875rem;line-height:1.25rem"><span style="display:block;padding:16px 0 0 16px;margin-bottom:-1px;width:100%;text-align:left;background-color:#fff"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="54" height="14" viewBox="0 0 54 14"><g fill="none" fill-rule="evenodd" transform="translate(1 1)"><circle cx="6" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FF5F56" stroke="#E0443E" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="26" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FFBD2E" stroke="#DEA123" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="46" cy="6" r="6" fill="#27C93F" stroke="#1AAB29" stroke-width=".5"></circle></g></svg></span><span role="button" tabindex="0" data-code="-num" style="color:#24292e;display:none" aria-label="Copy" class="code-block-pro-copy-button"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="width:24px;height:24px" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path class="with-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m-6 9l2 2 4-4"></path><path class="without-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2"></path></svg></span><pre class="shiki github-light" style="background-color: #fff" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="color: #D73A49">-</span><span style="color: #24292E">num</span></span></code></pre></div>
<!-- /wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>-19</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The unitary operator __abs__ defines the behaviour of the builtins function abs. The returned number is stripped of the sign:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"abs(num)","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003eabs\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e(num)\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>19</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The unitary operator __invert__ returns the ones complement:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"~num","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e~\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003enum\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>-20</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>If the ones complement is assigned to a variable:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Then num and complement can be converted to bytes and displayed in hex:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>'0013'</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"inverted.to_bytes(length=2, byteorder='big', signed=True).hex()","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003einverted.to_bytes(\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #E36209\u0022\u003elength\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003e2\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e, \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #E36209\u0022\u003ebyteorder\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #032F62\u0022\u003e\u0026#39;big\u0026#39;\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e, \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #E36209\u0022\u003esigned\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003eTrue\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e).hex()\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->

<!-- wp:preformatted -->
<pre class="wp-block-preformatted">'ffec'</pre>
<!-- /wp:preformatted -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Essentially the following hex characters are switched in the hex complement:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:table {"className":"is-style-stripes"} -->
<figure class="wp-block-table is-style-stripes"><table><tbody><tr><td>hex</td><td>hex complement</td></tr><tr><td>0</td><td>f</td></tr><tr><td>1</td><td>e</td></tr><tr><td>2</td><td>d</td></tr><tr><td>3</td><td>c</td></tr><tr><td>4</td><td>b</td></tr><tr><td>5</td><td>a</td></tr><tr><td>6</td><td>9</td></tr><tr><td>7</td><td>8</td></tr></tbody></table></figure>
<!-- /wp:table -->

<!-- wp:heading -->
<h2 class="wp-block-heading" id="rounding-data-model-identifiers">Rounding Data Model Identifiers</h2>
<!-- /wp:heading -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The data model identifiers __round__, __floor__, __ceil__, __trunc__ define the behaviour behind the builtins function round and the math functions ceil, floor and trunc. These rounding functions are used to round other numeric data types to an integer and in the case of an integer just return a copy of the integer.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"round(num)","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003eround\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e(num)\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->
<div class="wp-block-kevinbatdorf-code-block-pro" style="font-size:.875rem;line-height:1.25rem"><span style="display:block;padding:16px 0 0 16px;margin-bottom:-1px;width:100%;text-align:left;background-color:#fff"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="54" height="14" viewBox="0 0 54 14"><g fill="none" fill-rule="evenodd" transform="translate(1 1)"><circle cx="6" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FF5F56" stroke="#E0443E" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="26" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FFBD2E" stroke="#DEA123" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="46" cy="6" r="6" fill="#27C93F" stroke="#1AAB29" stroke-width=".5"></circle></g></svg></span><span role="button" tabindex="0" data-code="round(num)" style="color:#24292e;display:none" aria-label="Copy" class="code-block-pro-copy-button"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="width:24px;height:24px" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path class="with-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m-6 9l2 2 4-4"></path><path class="without-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2"></path></svg></span><pre class="shiki github-light" style="background-color: #fff" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="color: #005CC5">round</span><span style="color: #24292E">(num)</span></span></code></pre></div>

<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>19</code></pre>

<!-- wp:heading -->
<h2 class="wp-block-heading" id="casting-data-model-identifiers">Casting Data Model Identifiers</h2>
<!-- /wp:heading -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The __int__ data model identifier defines the behaviour when an integer is cast to an integer using the builtins int class. Since it is originally an integer, the returned integer has the same value:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"int(num)","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003eint\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e(num)\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->
<div class="wp-block-kevinbatdorf-code-block-pro" style="font-size:.875rem;line-height:1.25rem"><span style="display:block;padding:16px 0 0 16px;margin-bottom:-1px;width:100%;text-align:left;background-color:#fff"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="54" height="14" viewBox="0 0 54 14"><g fill="none" fill-rule="evenodd" transform="translate(1 1)"><circle cx="6" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FF5F56" stroke="#E0443E" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="26" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FFBD2E" stroke="#DEA123" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="46" cy="6" r="6" fill="#27C93F" stroke="#1AAB29" stroke-width=".5"></circle></g></svg></span><span role="button" tabindex="0" data-code="int(num)" style="color:#24292e;display:none" aria-label="Copy" class="code-block-pro-copy-button"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="width:24px;height:24px" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path class="with-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m-6 9l2 2 4-4"></path><path class="without-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2"></path></svg></span><pre class="shiki github-light" style="background-color: #fff" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="color: #005CC5">int</span><span style="color: #24292E">(num)</span></span></code></pre></div>
<!-- /wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>19</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The __bool__ data model identifier defines the behaviour when an integer is cast to a bool using the builtins bool class. All non-zero values are True and a zero value is False:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"bool(num)","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003ebool\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e(num)\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->
<div class="wp-block-kevinbatdorf-code-block-pro" style="font-size:.875rem;line-height:1.25rem"><span style="display:block;padding:16px 0 0 16px;margin-bottom:-1px;width:100%;text-align:left;background-color:#fff"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="54" height="14" viewBox="0 0 54 14"><g fill="none" fill-rule="evenodd" transform="translate(1 1)"><circle cx="6" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FF5F56" stroke="#E0443E" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="26" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FFBD2E" stroke="#DEA123" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="46" cy="6" r="6" fill="#27C93F" stroke="#1AAB29" stroke-width=".5"></circle></g></svg></span><span role="button" tabindex="0" data-code="bool(num)" style="color:#24292e;display:none" aria-label="Copy" class="code-block-pro-copy-button"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="width:24px;height:24px" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path class="with-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m-6 9l2 2 4-4"></path><path class="without-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2"></path></svg></span><pre class="shiki github-light" style="background-color: #fff" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="color: #005CC5">bool</span><span style="color: #24292E">(num)</span></span></code></pre></div>
<!-- /wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>True</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The __float__ data model identifier defines the behaviour when an integer is cast to a float using the builtins float class. Notice the inclusion of the decimal point in the output:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"float(num)","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003efloat\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e(num)\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->
<div class="wp-block-kevinbatdorf-code-block-pro" style="font-size:.875rem;line-height:1.25rem"><span style="display:block;padding:16px 0 0 16px;margin-bottom:-1px;width:100%;text-align:left;background-color:#fff"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="54" height="14" viewBox="0 0 54 14"><g fill="none" fill-rule="evenodd" transform="translate(1 1)"><circle cx="6" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FF5F56" stroke="#E0443E" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="26" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FFBD2E" stroke="#DEA123" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="46" cy="6" r="6" fill="#27C93F" stroke="#1AAB29" stroke-width=".5"></circle></g></svg></span><span role="button" tabindex="0" data-code="float(num)" style="color:#24292e;display:none" aria-label="Copy" class="code-block-pro-copy-button"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="width:24px;height:24px" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path class="with-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m-6 9l2 2 4-4"></path><path class="without-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2"></path></svg></span><pre class="shiki github-light" style="background-color: #fff" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="color: #005CC5">float</span><span style="color: #24292E">(num)</span></span></code></pre></div>
<!-- /wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>19.0</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:heading -->
<h2 class="wp-block-heading" id="binary-data-model-identifiers">Binary Data Model Identifiers</h2>
<!-- /wp:heading -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Binary data model identifiers are designed to work between two instances. </p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:table {"className":"is-style-stripes"} -->
<figure class="wp-block-table is-style-stripes"><table><tbody><tr><td>Data Model Identifier</td><td>Operator or Builtins</td></tr><tr><td>__add__</td><td>+</td></tr><tr><td>__sub__</td><td>-</td></tr><tr><td>__mul__</td><td>*</td></tr><tr><td>__pow__</td><td>**</td></tr><tr><td>__floordiv__</td><td>//</td></tr><tr><td>__mod__</td><td>%</td></tr><tr><td>__divmod__</td><td>divmod</td></tr><tr><td>__truediv__</td><td>/</td></tr></tbody></table></figure>
<!-- /wp:table -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The instance the operator is called from is known as <em>self</em> and the other instance is known as <em>value</em>. If the data model identifier was to be called directly it would be used with the following syntax:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"self.__add__(value)","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003eself\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e.\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003e__add__\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e(value)\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->
<div class="wp-block-kevinbatdorf-code-block-pro" style="font-size:.875rem;line-height:1.25rem"><span style="display:block;padding:16px 0 0 16px;margin-bottom:-1px;width:100%;text-align:left;background-color:#fff"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="54" height="14" viewBox="0 0 54 14"><g fill="none" fill-rule="evenodd" transform="translate(1 1)"><circle cx="6" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FF5F56" stroke="#E0443E" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="26" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FFBD2E" stroke="#DEA123" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="46" cy="6" r="6" fill="#27C93F" stroke="#1AAB29" stroke-width=".5"></circle></g></svg></span><span role="button" tabindex="0" data-code="self.__add__(value)" style="color:#24292e;display:none" aria-label="Copy" class="code-block-pro-copy-button"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="width:24px;height:24px" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path class="with-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m-6 9l2 2 4-4"></path><path class="without-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2"></path></svg></span><pre class="shiki github-light" style="background-color: #fff" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="color: #005CC5">self</span><span style="color: #24292E">.</span><span style="color: #005CC5">__add__</span><span style="color: #24292E">(value)</span></span></code></pre></div>
<!-- /wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>More typically, the operator is used:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"self + value","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003eself\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e+\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e value\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->
<div class="wp-block-kevinbatdorf-code-block-pro" style="font-size:.875rem;line-height:1.25rem"><span style="display:block;padding:16px 0 0 16px;margin-bottom:-1px;width:100%;text-align:left;background-color:#fff"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="54" height="14" viewBox="0 0 54 14"><g fill="none" fill-rule="evenodd" transform="translate(1 1)"><circle cx="6" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FF5F56" stroke="#E0443E" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="26" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FFBD2E" stroke="#DEA123" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="46" cy="6" r="6" fill="#27C93F" stroke="#1AAB29" stroke-width=".5"></circle></g></svg></span><span role="button" tabindex="0" data-code="self + value" style="color:#24292e;display:none" aria-label="Copy" class="code-block-pro-copy-button"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="width:24px;height:24px" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path class="with-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m-6 9l2 2 4-4"></path><path class="without-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2"></path></svg></span><pre class="shiki github-light" style="background-color: #fff" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="color: #005CC5">self</span><span style="color: #24292E"> </span><span style="color: #D73A49">+</span><span style="color: #24292E"> value</span></span></code></pre></div>
<!-- /wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Notice the instance the method is being called from <em>self</em> is on the left hand side of the operator and the other instance value is on the <em>right</em> hand side. There are a number of reverse data model methods which complement the above and describe what to do when the order is reversed:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:table {"className":"is-style-stripes"} -->
<figure class="wp-block-table is-style-stripes"><table><tbody><tr><td>Data Model Identifier</td><td>Reverse Data Model Identifier</td></tr><tr><td>__add__</td><td>__radd__</td></tr><tr><td>__sub__</td><td>__rsub__</td></tr><tr><td>__mul__</td><td>__rmul__</td></tr><tr><td>__pow__</td><td>__rpow__</td></tr><tr><td>__floordiv__</td><td>__rfloordiv__</td></tr><tr><td>__mod__</td><td>__rmod__</td></tr><tr><td>__divmod__</td><td>__rdivmod__</td></tr><tr><td>__truediv__</td><td>__rtruediv__</td></tr></tbody></table></figure>
<!-- /wp:table -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The reverse data model identifiers are typically invoked when the instances surrounding the operator are different class types. For example an integer can be used to replicate a string. The int data model identifier __mul__ will be used for the following operation (<em>self</em> is 2 and is on the left hand side of the * operator):</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"2 * 'hello'","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003e2\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e*\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #032F62\u0022\u003e\u0026#39;hello\u0026#39;\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->
<div class="wp-block-kevinbatdorf-code-block-pro" style="font-size:.875rem;line-height:1.25rem"><span style="display:block;padding:16px 0 0 16px;margin-bottom:-1px;width:100%;text-align:left;background-color:#fff"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="54" height="14" viewBox="0 0 54 14"><g fill="none" fill-rule="evenodd" transform="translate(1 1)"><circle cx="6" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FF5F56" stroke="#E0443E" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="26" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FFBD2E" stroke="#DEA123" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="46" cy="6" r="6" fill="#27C93F" stroke="#1AAB29" stroke-width=".5"></circle></g></svg></span><span role="button" tabindex="0" data-code="2 * 'hello'" style="color:#24292e;display:none" aria-label="Copy" class="code-block-pro-copy-button"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="width:24px;height:24px" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path class="with-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m-6 9l2 2 4-4"></path><path class="without-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2"></path></svg></span><pre class="shiki github-light" style="background-color: #fff" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="color: #005CC5">2</span><span style="color: #24292E"> </span><span style="color: #D73A49">*</span><span style="color: #24292E"> </span><span style="color: #032F62">&#39;hello&#39;</span></span></code></pre></div>
<!-- /wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>'hellohello'</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The int data model operator __rmul__ will instead be used for the following operation (<em>self</em> is 2 and is on the right hand side of the * operator):</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"'hello' * 2","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #032F62\u0022\u003e\u0026#39;hello\u0026#39;\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e*\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003e2\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->

<!-- /wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>'hellohello'</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>To use these, two instances will need to be created:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"num1 = 19\nnum2 = 52","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003enum1 \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003e19\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003enum2 \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003e52\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->

<!-- /wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Addition of two integers can be returned:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"num1 + num2","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003enum1 \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e+\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e num2\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>And therefore, the following equals num2:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The divmod of two integers returns a tuple containing the integer division and modulo:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"divmod(num2, num1)","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003edivmod\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e(num2, num1)\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->

<!-- /wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>(2, 14)</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Float Division of two integers will always return a floating point number, even if there is no Modulo with the integer division:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"num2 / num1","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003enum2 \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e/\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e num1\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->
<div class="wp-block-kevinbatdorf-code-block-pro" style="font-size:.875rem;line-height:1.25rem"><span style="display:block;padding:16px 0 0 16px;margin-bottom:-1px;width:100%;text-align:left;background-color:#fff"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="54" height="14" viewBox="0 0 54 14"><g fill="none" fill-rule="evenodd" transform="translate(1 1)"><circle cx="6" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FF5F56" stroke="#E0443E" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="26" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FFBD2E" stroke="#DEA123" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="46" cy="6" r="6" fill="#27C93F" stroke="#1AAB29" stroke-width=".5"></circle></g></svg></span><span role="button" tabindex="0" data-code="num2 / num1" style="color:#24292e;display:none" aria-label="Copy" class="code-block-pro-copy-button"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="width:24px;height:24px" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path class="with-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m-6 9l2 2 4-4"></path><path class="without-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2"></path></svg></span><pre class="shiki github-light" style="background-color: #fff" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="color: #24292E">num2 </span><span style="color: #D73A49">/</span><span style="color: #24292E"> num1</span></span></code></pre></div>
<!-- /wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>2.736842105263158</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:heading -->
<h2 class="wp-block-heading" id="binary-bitwise-data-model-operators">Binary Bitwise Data Model Operators</h2>
<!-- /wp:heading -->

<!-- wp:table {"className":"is-style-stripes"} -->
<figure class="wp-block-table is-style-stripes"><table><tbody><tr><td>Data Model Identifier</td><td>Operator</td></tr><tr><td>__lshift__</td><td>&lt;&lt;</td></tr><tr><td>__rshift__</td><td>&gt;&gt;</td></tr><tr><td>__and__</td><td>&amp;</td></tr><tr><td>__or__</td><td>|</td></tr><tr><td>__xor__</td><td>^</td></tr></tbody></table></figure>
<!-- /wp:table -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The int num1 can be examined in binary:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"num1 = 19","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003enum1 \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003e19\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>'0b10011'</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>If it is right shifted by two places, the two least significant digits which were 11 are removed:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"bin(num1 \u003e\u003e 2)","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003ebin\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e(num1 \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e\u0026gt;\u0026gt;\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003e2\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e)\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->

<!-- /wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>'0b100'</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>This gives the integer:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"num1 \u003e\u003e num2","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003enum1 \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e\u0026gt;\u0026gt;\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e num2\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>1</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>If num1 is examined in binary again:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"bin(num1)","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003ebin\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e(num1)\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->
<div class="wp-block-kevinbatdorf-code-block-pro" style="font-size:.875rem;line-height:1.25rem"><span style="display:block;padding:16px 0 0 16px;margin-bottom:-1px;width:100%;text-align:left;background-color:#fff"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="54" height="14" viewBox="0 0 54 14"><g fill="none" fill-rule="evenodd" transform="translate(1 1)"><circle cx="6" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FF5F56" stroke="#E0443E" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="26" cy="6" r="6" fill="#FFBD2E" stroke="#DEA123" stroke-width=".5"></circle><circle cx="46" cy="6" r="6" fill="#27C93F" stroke="#1AAB29" stroke-width=".5"></circle></g></svg></span><span role="button" tabindex="0" data-code="bin(num1)" style="color:#24292e;display:none" aria-label="Copy" class="code-block-pro-copy-button"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="width:24px;height:24px" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path class="with-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m-6 9l2 2 4-4"></path><path class="without-check" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M9 5H7a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2h-2M9 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M9 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2"></path></svg></span><pre class="shiki github-light" style="background-color: #fff" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="color: #005CC5">bin</span><span style="color: #24292E">(num1)</span></span></code></pre></div>
<!-- /wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>'0b10011'</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>And instead is left-shifted by two places</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"bin(num1 \u0026lt;\u0026lt; num2)","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003ebin\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e(num1 \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e\u0026lt;\u0026lt;\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e num2)\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>'0b1001100'</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>This gives the integer:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>76</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The bitwise operator &amp; will return an integer that has a bit of 1 when both respective bits in the instance num1 and num2 are 1 and is 0 otherwise.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>This can be seen when the following two integers are created:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>In this example on the first two bits are 1 in num1 and num2:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"num1 \u0026amp; num2","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003enum1 \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e\u0026amp;\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e num2\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>192</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The bitwise operator or will return an integer that has a bit of 1 when either bits in the instance num1 and num2 are 1 and is only 0 when both are 0. The binary sequence of each number can be examined:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"bin(num1)","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003ebin\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e(num1)\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Then the bitwise or operator can be examined, only the third and sixth position are 0 as the corresponding bit is 0 in num1 and num2:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>This corresponds to the integer:</p>

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Finally the exclusive or operator will return an integer that has a bit of 1 when the bits in the instance num1 and num2 are different and otherwise has a bit of 0. The binary sequence of each number can be examined:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The first three leading bits are 0 and aren't shown:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->
