<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"num1 ^ num2","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003enum1 \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e^\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e num2\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->

<!-- /wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>27</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>These operators also have reverse equivalents:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:table {"className":"is-style-stripes"} -->
<figure class="wp-block-table is-style-stripes"><table><tbody><tr><td>Data Model Identifier</td><td>Reverse Data Model Identifier</td></tr><tr><td>__lshift__</td><td>__rlshift__</td></tr><tr><td>__rshift__</td><td>__rrshift__</td></tr><tr><td>__and__</td><td>__rand__</td></tr><tr><td>__or__</td><td>__ror__</td></tr><tr><td>__xor__</td><td>__rxor__</td></tr></tbody></table></figure>
<!-- /wp:table -->

<!-- wp:heading -->
<h2 class="wp-block-heading" id="binary-comparison-data-model-identifiers">Binary Comparison Data Model Identifiers</h2>
<!-- /wp:heading -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Since integers are ordinal, the 6 comparison operators are configured:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:table {"className":"is-style-stripes"} -->
<figure class="wp-block-table is-style-stripes"><table><tbody><tr><td>Data Model Identifier </td><td>Operator</td></tr><tr><td>__eq__</td><td>==</td></tr><tr><td>__ne__</td><td>!=</td></tr><tr><td>__gt__</td><td>&gt;</td></tr><tr><td>__lt__</td><td>&lt;</td></tr><tr><td>__ge__</td><td>&gt;=</td></tr><tr><td>__le__</td><td>&lt;=</td></tr></tbody></table></figure>
<!-- /wp:table -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>These 6 comparison operators can be used to compare two integers returning a boolean value of True, if the statement is True, otherwise returning a boolean value of False.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>A check can be made to see if num1 is less than or equal to num2:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"num1 \u0026lt;= num2","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003enum1 \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e\u0026lt;=\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e num2\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>True</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:heading -->
<h2 class="wp-block-heading" id="pedmas">PEDMAS</h2>
<!-- /wp:heading -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>When multiple binary operators are used, a calculation is no carried out from left to right, instead there is a preference for operations in the form of PEDMAS:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:table {"className":"is-style-stripes"} -->
<figure class="wp-block-table is-style-stripes"><table><tbody><tr><td>Precidence</td><td>Operator</td></tr><tr><td>1. <strong>P</strong>arenthesis</td><td>( )</td></tr><tr><td>2. <strong>E</strong>xponentiation</td><td>**</td></tr><tr><td>3. <strong>D</strong>ivision</td><td>/ or // or %</td></tr><tr><td>4. <strong>M</strong>ultiplication</td><td>*</td></tr><tr><td>5. <strong>A</strong>ddition</td><td>+</td></tr><tr><td>6. <strong>S</strong>ubtraction</td><td>-</td></tr></tbody></table></figure>
<!-- /wp:table -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The effect of PEDMAS can be seen in the following:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:kevinbatdorf/code-block-pro {"code":"1 + 2 - 3 * 4 ** 5","codeHTML":"\u003cpre class=\u0022shiki github-light\u0022 style=\u0022background-color: #fff\u0022 tabindex=\u00220\u0022\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\u0022line\u0022\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003e1\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e+\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003e2\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e-\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003e3\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e*\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003e4\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #D73A49\u0022\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #24292E\u0022\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\u0022color: #005CC5\u0022\u003e5\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","language":"python","theme":"github-light","bgColor":"#fff","textColor":"#24292e","fontSize":".875rem","lineHeight":"1.25rem","headerType":"headlights","seeMoreString":"","seeMoreAfterLine":"","seeMoreTransition":false,"lineHighlightColor":"rgba(16, 41, 67, 0.2)","copyButton":true} -->

<!-- wp:code -->
<pre class="wp-block-code"><code>-3069</code></pre>
<!-- /wp:code -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>This is done using the exponentiation first:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Then the multiplication:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Then the addition and subtraction have the same order of precedence:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Then the operation in the brackets is carried out first giving 0 and anything multiplied by 0 is 0.</p>
